agent={updated:j.updated,rotation:j.rotation,alerts:j.alerts}; localStorage.setItem('j1_agent',JSON.stringify(agent));saveMeta(); msg.innerHTML='<span style="color:#10b981">???лЁҜм” ?кҫӘл“ғ ?кі—м” ???кіёмҠң??/span>';sxRender(); }catch(e){msg.innerHTML='<span style="color:#f5604d">???г…ҪлҷЈ: '+e.message+' (URLмЁҢжҖЁл“Ұм»»?Сү? ?ләӨм”Ө)</span>';} }; /* ---- init after JACK1 loads ---- */ window.addEventListener('load',function(){setTimeout(injectTab,300);}); })(); </script> </body> </html>
